           $(document).ready(function () {
        //var retUrl = "/en-us/evalcenter/account/ExternalLoginCallback?returnUrl=" + window.location.pathname;//location.href.replace(/(.+\w\/)(.+)/, "/$2")
        var loginUrlNew = "/en-us/evalcenter/account/externallogin?ReturnUrl=" + escape(window.location);
        $('form').each(function (selindex) {
            var actionToReplace = $(this).attr("action");
            if (actionToReplace.toLowerCase().indexOf("externallogin") != -1) {
                $(this).attr("action",loginUrlNew);
            }
        });
    });
    function InvokeMicrosoftSignIn() {
        var loginUrlNew = "/en-us/evalcenter/account/externallogin?ReturnUrl=" + escape(window.location);
        $('form').each(function (selindex) {
            var actionToReplace = $(this).attr("action");
            if (actionToReplace.toLowerCase().indexOf("externallogin") != -1) {
                $(this).attr("action", loginUrlNew);
            }
        });
        document.getElementById('btnMicrosoftSignIn').value = Modernizr.mq('(max-width: 767px)'); //isMobile
        document.getElementById('btnMicrosoftSignIn').click();
    }
          </script>

              <div class="stepContent panel-collapse collapse" id="description_1592">
               <div class="accordion-inner descriptionInfo">
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  With optional Windows Server 2012 R2
                 </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                 System Center 2012 R2 delivers unified management across on-premises, service provider and Microsoft Azure environments, in a manner thats simple and cost-effective, application focused, and enterprise-class. System Center 2012 R2 offers exciting new features and enhancements across infrastructure provisioning, infrastructure monitoring, application performance monitoring, automation &amp; self-service, and IT service management.
                </p>
                <p>
                 Need more information about System Center 2012 R2? See the
                 <a href="http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/server-cloud/system-center/system-center-2012-r2.aspx" target="_blank">
                  product details page.
                 </a>
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  Languages
                 </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Chinese (Simplified), English, French, German, Spanish, Italian, Japanese, Russian
                </p>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  Benefits
                 </strong>
                </p>
                <ul>
                 <li>
                  <strong>
                   Hybrid IT:
                  </strong>
                  Consistent with the notion of the Microsoft Cloud Platform, hybrid is built into System Center. System Center truly enables common management that spans Windows Server and Windows Azure environments, be it provisioning, self-service, monitoring, or IT service management.
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  <strong>
                   Enterprise-class:
                  </strong>
                  System Center infrastructure management capabilities are enterprise grade and ready to use today. Not only is System Center best-of-breed for Windows environments and Microsoft workloads (like Exchange, SharePoint and SQL) but it also enables robust management of heterogeneous datacenters.
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  <strong>
                   Reduce datacenter complexity:
                  </strong>
                  Were constantly striving to reduce complexity in your datacenter by making it easy to provision, manage and operate infrastructure services with System Center.
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  <strong>
                   Application focused:
                  </strong>
                  System Center has a relentless focus on optimizing your apps and workloads by arming you with rich insights to help you deliver predictable application SLA (after all, apps are what your business cares about and infrastructure exists to support them).
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <p>
                 <strong>
                  Edition
                 </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                 System Center 2012 R2 Datacenter |64-bit .exe
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 Note: This evaluation includes System Center 2012 R2 Configuration Manager SP1 and System Center 2012 R2 Endpoint Protection SP1. System Center 2012 R2 Configuration Manager SP1 and System Center 2012 R2 Endpoint Protection SP1 are provided as a single installation package.
                </p>
